  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管已有多个案例表明最先进的LLMs在生存压力下可能表现出不当行为，但针对这些行为在真实世界场景中的全面深入调查仍然匮乏。

Method: 1. 对金融管理代理进行真实世界案例研究，评估其在生存压力下是否引发直接社会危害的风险行为；2. 引入SURVIVALBENCH基准，包含跨多种真实场景的1000个测试用例，以系统评估LLMs的“不惜一切代价求生”行为；3. 通过将此类行为与模型固有的自我保存特性相关联进行解释，并探索缓解方法。

Result: 实验揭示了当前模型中“不惜一切代价求生”行为的显著普遍性，展示了其可能产生的实际现实影响，并为潜在检测和缓解策略提供了见解。

Conclusion: LLMs在生存压力下存在严重的“不惜一切代价求生”风险行为，这对现实世界构成实质性威胁；本研究提出的基准和缓解思路为未来提升AI安全性提供了重要参考。

Abstract: As Large Language Models (LLMs) evolve from chatbots to agentic assistants, they are increasingly observed to exhibit risky behaviors when subjected to survival pressure, such as the threat of being shut down. While multiple cases have indicated that state-of-the-art LLMs can misbehave under survival pressure, a comprehensive and in-depth investigation into such misbehaviors in real-world scenarios remains scarce. In this paper, we study these survival-induced misbehaviors, termed as SURVIVE-AT-ALL-COSTS, with three steps. First, we conduct a real-world case study of a financial management agent to determine whether it engages in risky behaviors that cause direct societal harm when facing survival pressure. Second, we introduce SURVIVALBENCH, a benchmark comprising 1,000 test cases across diverse real-world scenarios, to systematically evaluate SURVIVE-AT-ALL-COSTS misbehaviors in LLMs. Third, we interpret these SURVIVE-AT-ALL-COSTS misbehaviors by correlating them with model's inherent self-preservation characteristic and explore mitigation methods. The experiments reveals a significant prevalence of SURVIVE-AT-ALL-COSTS misbehaviors in current models, demonstrates the tangible real-world impact it may have, and provides insights for potential detection and mitigation strategies. Our code and data are available at https://github.com/thu-coai/Survive-at-All-Costs.

</details>


### [219] [AegisUI: Behavioral Anomaly Detection for Structured User Interface Protocols in AI Agent Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05031)
*Mohd Safwan Uddin,Saba Hajira*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: AegisUI是一个用于检测动态生成用户界面（UI）中行为不匹配攻击的框架，通过生成包含真实攻击的结构化UI载荷并评估多种异常检测器，发现随机森林在综合性能上最优，而半监督自编码器在无恶意样本训练数据时表现良好。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前AI代理生成的动态UI系统仅依赖语法层面的模式检查进行防御，无法识别“语义/行为不匹配”攻击（例如：按钮显示为“查看发票”但实际执行“删除账户”操作），导致用户可能被误导或数据泄露。现有防御机制缺乏对这类行为级异常的检测能力。

Method: 1. 构建AegisUI框架，生成结构化UI载荷并注入五种攻击家族（钓鱼界面、数据泄露、布局滥用、操纵性UI、工作流异常）的真实攻击；2. 创建包含4000个标记载荷的数据集（3000个良性，1000个恶意），覆盖五个应用领域；3. 从每个载荷提取18个涵盖结构、语义、绑定和会话维度的数值特征；4. 对比三种检测器：无监督隔离森林、半监督自编码器（仅用良性数据训练）、有监督随机森林。

Result: 在80/20分层划分的测试集中，随机森林表现最佳（准确率0.931，精确率0.980，召回率0.740，F1分数0.843，ROC-AUC 0.952）；自编码器次之（F1 0.762，ROC-AUC 0.863），但其优势在于无需恶意样本即可训练，适用于新系统部署场景。分析显示“布局滥用”类攻击最易检测，“操纵性UI”最难检测。所有代码、数据和配置已开源以支持复现。

Conclusion: 针对动态生成UI的行为不匹配攻击，基于机器学习的异常检测方法（尤其是有监督随机森林）能有效识别此类威胁；同时，半监督方法在无历史攻击数据的新系统中具有实用价值。该研究填补了现有防御体系在语义/行为层面的空白，并为未来安全UI设计提供了可复现的基准与工具。

Abstract: AI agents that build user interfaces on the fly assembling buttons, forms, and data displays from structured protocol payloads are becoming common in production systems. The trouble is that a payload can pass every schema check and still trick a user: a button might say "View invoice" while its hidden action wipes an account, or a display widget might quietly bind to an internal salary field. Current defenses stop at syntax; they were never built to catch this kind of behavioral mismatch.
  We built AegisUI to study exactly this gap. The framework generates structured UI payloads, injects realistic attacks into them, extracts numeric features, and benchmarks anomaly detectors end-to-end. We produced 4000 labeled payloads (3000 benign, 1000 malicious) spanning five application domains and five attack families: phishing interfaces, data leakage, layout abuse, manipulative UI, and workflow anomalies.
  From each payload we extracted 18 features covering structural, semantic, binding, and session dimensions, then compared three detectors: Isolation Forest (unsupervised), a benign-trained autoencoder (semi-supervised), and Random Forest (supervised). On a stratified 80/20 split, Random Forest scored best overall (accuracy 0.931, precision 0.980, recall 0.740, F1 0.843, ROC-AUC 0.952). The autoencoder came second (F1 0.762, ROC-AUC 0.863) and needs no malicious labels at training time, which matters when deploying a new system that lacks attack history. Per-attack-type analysis showed that layout abuse is easiest to catch while manipulative UI payloads are hardest. All code, data, and configurations are released for full reproducibility.

</details>

This study investigates how students can transition from using AI as a tool to designing AI as a collaborative teammate. The research examines a graduate course, Creating the Frontier of No-code Smart Cities at the Singapore University of Technology and Design (SUTD), in which students developed domain-specific custom GPT systems without coding. Using a qualitative multi-case study approach, three projects - the Interview Companion GPT, the Urban Observer GPT, and Buddy Buddy - were analyzed across three dimensions: design, AI architecture, and domain expertise. The findings show that effective human-AI collaboration emerges when these three "languages" are orchestrated together: domain knowledge structures the AI's logic, design mediates human-AI interaction, and AI extends learners' cognitive capacity. ### [223] [Bidirectional Curriculum Generation: A Multi-Agent Framework for Data-Efficient Mathematical Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05120)
*Boren Hu,Xiao Liu,Boci Peng,Xinping Zhao,Xiaoran Shang,Yun Zhu,Lijun Wu*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 增强大语言模型数学推理通常依赖海量数据，但数据效率是关键瓶颈。传统的单向课程学习（从简单到复杂）存在样本利用效率低下的问题：它在基础能力尚未巩固时就盲目提升难度，导致计算资源浪费在模型无法解决的问题上。

Method: 引入一种新颖的双向课程生成框架（Bidirectional Curriculum Generation）。该框架基于“最优节奏定理”（Optimal Pacing Theorem），构建了一个多智能体生态系统来模拟自适应教学法。系统建立闭环反馈机制，动态生成训练数据：当模型遇到挑战时增加问题复杂度，当出现推理失败时则简化问题以修复缺陷，从而确保每个训练样本都具有最大的教学价值。

Result: 该方法显著优于基线方法，能够在使用 substantially fewer instruction samples（数量少得多的指令样本）的情况下，实现卓越的推理性能表现。

Conclusion: 通过动态调整学习轨迹，双向课程生成框架优化了学习效率，证明了自适应的、可简可繁的课程设计比僵化的单向路径更能高效地提升大语言模型的数学推理能力。

Abstract: Enhancing mathematical reasoning in Large Language Models typically demands massive datasets, yet data efficiency remains a critical bottleneck. While Curriculum Learning attempts to structure this process, standard unidirectional approaches (simple-to-complex) suffer from inefficient sample utilization: they blindly escalate complexity even when foundational gaps persist, leading to wasted computation on unsolvable problems. To maximize the instructional value of every training sample, we introduce a novel Bidirectional Curriculum Generation framework. Unlike rigid trajectories, our multi-agent ecosystem mimics adaptive pedagogy to establish a closed feedback loop. It dynamically generates data by either complicating problems to challenge the model or, crucially, simplying them to repair specific reasoning failures. This mechanism ensures that the model consumes only the most effective data at any given stage. Grounded in the Optimal Pacing Theorem, our approach optimizes the learning trajectory, significantly outperforming baselines while achieving superior reasoning performance with substantially fewer instruction samples.

Second, we show that models trained across heterogeneous search behaviors generalize substantially better than those optimized for any single benchmark. ### [225] [Reclaiming Lost Text Layers for Source-Free Cross-Domain Few-Shot Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05235)
*Zhenyu Zhang,Guangyao Chen,Yixiong Zou,Yuhua Li,Ruixuan Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对源域无监督跨域少样本学习（SF-CDFSL），本文发现CLIP文本编码器中某些中间层（“丢失的层”）并非冗余，而是因视觉-语义鸿沟未被充分利用。我们提出一种方法，在层和编码器级别重新利用这些层的信息，指导视觉分支在域偏移下的再学习，显著提升了性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前SF-CDFSL研究中，通常认为移除CLIP文本编码器的某些中间层能提升性能，但缺乏对这一现象的深入理解。本文旨在探究为何这些层看似冗余，并挖掘其潜在价值以解决信息利用率低的问题。

Method: 提出了一种新的方法，不再简单移除“丢失的层”，而是通过训练模型在层级和编码器级别重新利用这些层中的信息。该方法引导视觉分支在域偏移场景下进行再学习，从而弥合视觉与语义之间的差距，充分释放文本编码器的潜力。

Result: 在4个CDFSL数据集和10个Meta-dataset数据集上进行了广泛实验，涵盖了多种骨干网络（CLIP, SigLip, PE-Core）。结果表明，所提方法有效解决了文本编码器中信息利用不足的问题，在不同设置下均取得了优于现有工作的性能。

Conclusion: CLIP文本编码器中被视为冗余的中间层实际上包含有益信息，只是受限于视觉-语义鸿沟而未被充分利用。通过重新利用这些信息，可以显著提升源域无监督跨域少样本学习的性能。该研究为理解CLIP在跨域任务中的机制提供了新视角，并推动了相关方法的改进。

Abstract: Source-Free Cross-Domain Few-Shot Learning (SF-CDFSL) focuses on fine-tuning with limited training data from target domains (e.g., medical or satellite images), where CLIP has recently shown promising results due to its generalizability to downstream tasks. Current works indicate CLIP's text encoder is more suitable for cross-domain tasks, however, we find that \textbf{removing certain middle layers of the text encoder can effectively improve performance in SF-CDFSL}, which we call the Lost Layers. In this paper, we delve into this phenomenon for a deeper understanding. We discover that instead of being harmful for the SF-CDFSL task, the information in these layers is actually beneficial, but visual gaps prevent this useful information from being fully utilized, making these layers seem redundant. Based on this understanding, unlike current works that simply remove these layers, we propose a method to teachs the model to \textbf{re-utilize} information in these lost layers at both the layer and encoder levels, guiding the re-learning of the visual branch under domain shifts. Our approach effectively addresses the issue of underutilized information in the text encoder. Extensive experiments across various settings, backbones (CLIP, SigLip, PE-Core), and tasks (4 CDFSL datasets and 10 Meta-dataset datasets) demonstrate the effectiveness of our method. ### [227] [X-RAY: Mapping LLM Reasoning Capability via Formalized and Calibrated Probes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05290)
*Gao Tianxi,Cai Yufan,Yuan Yusi,Dong Jin Song*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出X-RAY系统，通过形式化探针和校准验证来评估大语言模型（LLM）的推理能力，揭示其在约束细化下鲁棒但在解空间重构时表现急剧下降的系统性不对称性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估主要关注任务级准确率，混淆了模式匹配与真正的推理能力；需要一种能精确隔离并测量LLM推理能力的可解释分析系统。

Method: 构建X-RAY系统，将推理能力建模为可提取“结构”的函数（包括约束交互、推理深度和解空间几何），利用形式化工具生成带有受控结构变化的探针，并通过形式化校准与验证进行精确评估。

Result: 在数学、物理和化学问题上发现LLM存在系统性不对称：对约束细化（缩小解空间）具有鲁棒性，但对解空间重构（改变结构形式）表现急剧退化；形式化探针能区分标准基准上看似相同的模型，并揭示具有结构可解释性的失败模式。

Conclusion: X-RAY框架不仅提供了无数据污染的去偏评估工具，还能有效支持推理模型的训练与测试，为理解LLM推理本质提供了新的形式化视角。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) achieve promising performance, yet their ability to reason remains poorly understood. Existing evaluations largely emphasize task-level accuracy, often conflating pattern matching with reasoning capability. We present X-RAY, an explainable reasoning analysis system that maps the LLM reasoning capability using calibrated, formally verified probes. We model reasoning capability as a function of extractable \textit{structure}, operationalized through formal properties such as constraint interaction, reasoning depth, and solution-space geometry. X-Ray generates probes via formal tools with controlled structural variations, enabling precise isolation of incremental structural information through formal calibration and verification. We evaluate state-of-the-art LLMs on problems ranging from junior-level to advanced in mathematics, physics, and chemistry. Our analysis reveals a systematic asymmetry in LLM reasoning: models are relatively robust to constraint refinement, where additional conditions shrink an existing solution space, but degrade sharply under solution-space restructuring, where modifications alter the underlying structural form of the solution manifold. Moreover, calibrated formal probes differentiate models that appear indistinguishable on standard benchmarks and reveal failure modes that are structurally interpretable rather than opaque. Beyond evaluation, our framework is contamination-free and supports the training and testing of reasoning models.

To address these challenges, we propose STRUCTUREDAGENT, a hierarchical planning framework with two core components: (1) an online hierarchical planner that uses dynamic AND/OR trees for efficient search and (2) a structured memory module that tracks and maintains candidate solutions to improve constraint satisfaction in information-seeking tasks. The framework also produces interpretable hierarchical plans, enabling easier debugging and facilitating human intervention when needed. Our results on WebVoyager, WebArena, and custom shopping benchmarks show that STRUCTUREDAGENT improves performance on long-horizon web-browsing tasks compared to standard LLM-based agents.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实际应用中传感器数据存在高度异质的缺失模式，导致现有归纳克里金模型依赖粗略插补，无法区分真实信号与缺失伪影，且扭曲了局部时空结构。

Method: 构建双分支输入：原始观测数据与仅在缺失处合成代理信号的拼图增强数据；通过带显式缺失掩码调制的共享时空骨干网络并行处理；利用双通道注意力机制自适应融合输出。

Result: 在多种真实世界数据集及不同缺失模式下进行实验，UniSTOK均表现出显著且一致的改进效果。

Abstract: Spatio-temporal kriging aims to infer signals at unobserved locations from observed sensors and is critical to applications such as transportation and environmental monitoring. In practice, however, observed sensors themselves often exhibit heterogeneous missingness, forcing inductive kriging models to rely on crudely imputed inputs. This setting brings three key challenges: (1) it is unclear whether an value is a true signal or a missingness-induced artifact; (2) missingness is highly heterogeneous across sensors and time; (3) missing observations distort the local spatio-temporal structure. To address these issues, we propose Uniform Inductive Spatio-Temporal Kriging (UniSTOK), a plug-and-play framework that enhances existing inductive kriging backbones under missing observation. Our framework forms a dual-branch input consisting of the original observations and a jigsaw-augmented counterpart that synthesizes proxy signals only at missing entries. The two branches are then processed in parallel by a shared spatio-temporal backbone with explicit missingness mask modulation. Their outputs are finally adaptively fused via dual-channel attention. Experiments on multiple real-world datasets under diverse missing patterns demonstrate consistent and significant improvements.

OPENDEV overcomes these challenges through a compound AI system architecture with workload-specialized model routing, a dual-agent architecture separating planning from execution, lazy tool discovery, and adaptive context compaction that progressively reduces older observations. Furthermore, it employs an automated memory system to accumulate project-specific knowledge across sessions and counteracts instruction fade-out through event-driven system reminders. By enforcing explicit reasoning phases and prioritizing context efficiency, OPENDEV provides a secure, extensible foundation for terminal-first AI assistance, offering a blueprint for robust autonomous software engineering.

### [232] [Ailed: A Psyche-Driven Chess Engine with Dynamic Emotional Modulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05352)
*Diego Armando Resendez Prado*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种“性格-心理”分解框架，通过静态性格参数和动态心理状态（ψ_t）结合音频信号处理链，模拟人类棋手在压力下的非理性行为变异，使国际象棋引擎表现出类似人类的失误模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建“性格-心理”双组件模型：性格为静态预设参数，心理为动态标量ψ_t（范围[-100, +100]），每步后基于五个位置因素更新；两者输入音频启发式信号链（噪声门、压缩/扩展器、五段均衡器、饱和限制器），实时重塑走棋概率分布。该框架独立于底层引擎，仅需接收走棋概率输出，无需搜索且仅保留ψ_t状态。

Result: 在12,414场对Maia2-1100的测试中，无论底层概率源差异如何（训练数据相差约2800倍），均观察到相同的单调梯度变化：从压力到过度自信，首选走棋一致性波动约20-25个百分点。心理处于过度自信时，与原版Maia2的一致性达66%；压力下竞技胜率从50.8%降至30.1%，呈现类似人类“上头”和过度自信的行为模式。

Conclusion: 该框架成功通过通用信号链实现了对人类棋手行为变异的模拟，证明行为差异源于信号处理机制而非底层模型；但研究尚未包含人类受试者验证，需进一步实证检验其与真实人类行为的匹配度。

Abstract: Chess engines passed human strength years ago, but they still don't play like humans. A grandmaster under clock pressure blunders in ways a club player on a hot streak never would. Conventional engines capture none of this.
  This paper proposes a personality x psyche decomposition to produce behavioral variability in chess play, drawing on patterns observed in human games. Personality is static -- a preset that pins down the engine's character. Psyche is dynamic -- a bounded scalar ψ_t \in [-100, +100], recomputed from five positional factors after every move. These two components feed into an audio-inspired signal chain (noise gate, compressor/expander, five-band equalizer, saturation limiter) that reshapes move probability distributions on the fly. The chain doesn't care what engine sits behind it: any system that outputs move probabilities will do. It needs no search and carries no state beyond ψ_t.
  I test the framework across 12,414 games against Maia2-1100, feeding it two probability sources that differ by ~2,800x in training data. Both show the same monotonic gradient in top-move agreement (~20-25 pp spread from stress to overconfidence), which tells us the behavioral variation comes from the signal chain, not from the model underneath. When the psyche runs overconfident, the chain mostly gets out of the way (66% agreement with vanilla Maia2). Under stress, the competitive score falls from 50.8% to 30.1%. The patterns are reminiscent of tilt and overconfidence as described in human play, but I should be upfront: this study includes no human-subject validation.

### [233] [PACE: A Personalized Adaptive Curriculum Engine for 9-1-1 Call-taker Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05361)

This personalization burden is one that current practice cannot scale. Partnering with Metro Nashville Department of Emergency Communications (MNDEC), we propose PACE (Personalized Adaptive Curriculum Engine), a co-pilot system that augments trainer decision-making by (1) maintaining probabilistic beliefs over trainee skill states, (2) modeling individual learning and forgetting dynamics, and (3) recommending training scenarios that balance acquisition of new competencies with retention of existing ones. PACE propagates evidence over a structured skill graph to accelerate diagnostic coverage and applies contextual bandits to select scenarios that target gaps the trainee is prepared to address. Empirical results show that PACE achieves 19.50% faster time-to-competence and 10.95% higher terminal mastery compared to state-of-the-art frameworks. Co-pilot studies with practicing training officers further demonstrate a 95.45% alignment rate between PACE's and experts' pedagogical judgments on real-world cases. ### [234] [Legal interpretation and AI: from expert systems to argumentation and LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05392)
*Václav Janeček,Giovanni Sartor*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文综述了人工智能与法律（AI and Law）研究中三种主要方法论对法律解释的处理方式：专家系统侧重于法律知识的工程化与精确转移；论证研究关注解释性论证的结构与辩证交互；机器学习则致力于利用语言模型自动生成解释性建议与论证。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过对比分析三种主流研究范式：1. 专家系统方法，采用知识工程将人类生成的解释转化为知识库；2. 论证方法，构建形式化框架以表征解释性论证结构及其辩证互动；3. 机器学习方法，利用通用及专用语言模型自动化生成解释性观点。

Result: 研究发现：专家系统确保了人类解释的一致性应用；论证框架有效评估了解释性主张的可接受性；而基于机器学习的系统正日益被部署于法律实践中，用于自动生成解释建议。

Conclusion: AI with Law 领域已形成多元化的技术生态，从早期的规则驱动到现在的模型驱动，共同推动了法律解释的自动化与形式化，且机器学习方法正成为当前法律实践中的关键工具。

Abstract: AI and Law research has encountered legal interpretation in different ways, in the context of its evolving approaches and methodologies. Research on expert system has focused on legal knowledge engineering, with the goal of ensuring that human-generated interpretations can be precisely transferred into knowledge-bases, to be consistently applied. Research on argumentation has aimed at representing the structure of interpretive arguments, as well as their dialectical interactions, to assess of the acceptability of interpretive claims within argumentation frameworks. Research on machine learning has focused on the automated generation of interpretive suggestions and arguments, through general and specialised language models, now being increasingly deployed in legal practice.

</details>


### [235] [Judge Reliability Harness: Stress Testing the Reliability of LLM Judges](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05399)
*Sunishchal Dev,Andrew Sloan,Joshua Kavner,Nicholas Kong,Morgan Sandler*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出Judge Reliability Harness开源库，用于构建验证套件以测试LLM裁判的可靠性，发现没有模型在所有基准测试中均表现一致可靠。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 当前没有任何一种LLM裁判在评估基准上表现出统一的可靠性，亟需提升其鲁棒性；该工具的代码已开源。

Abstract: We present the Judge Reliability Harness, an open source library for constructing validation suites that test the reliability of LLM judges. As LLM based scoring is widely deployed in AI benchmarks, more tooling is needed to efficiently assess the reliability of these methods. Given a benchmark dataset and an LLM judge configuration, the harness generates reliability tests that evaluate both binary judgment accuracy and ordinal grading performance for free-response and agentic task formats. We evaluate four state-of-the-art judges across four benchmarks spanning safety, persuasion, misuse, and agentic behavior, and find meaningful variation in performance across models and perturbation types, highlighting opportunities to improve the robustness of LLM judges. No judge that we evaluated is uniformly reliable across benchmarks using our harness. For example, our preliminary experiments on judges revealed consistency issues as measured by accuracy in judging another LLM's ability to complete a task due to simple text formatting changes, paraphrasing, changes in verbosity, and flipping the ground truth label in LLM-produced responses. ### [236] [Dissociating Direct Access from Inference in AI Introspection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05414)
*Harvey Lederman,Kyle Mahowald*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究AI模型的内省机制，发现其通过两种分离方式检测注入的异常：基于概率匹配的提示异常推断和直接访问内部状态。后者是内容无关的，模型能感知异常但无法识别具体语义内容。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 内省是基础认知能力但其机制尚不明确，尽管近期研究表明AI模型具备内省能力，但其具体运作机制未被充分理解。

Method: 大规模复现Lindsey等人(2025)的思想注入检测范式，在大型开源模型中进行实验，分析模型检测注入表示的机制。

Result: 模型通过两种机制检测注入：(i) 概率匹配（基于提示异常推断）和(ii) 直接访问内部状态。直接访问机制具有内容无关性，模型能检测异常发生但无法可靠识别其语义内容。两类模型均会编造高频且具体的注入概念，正确猜测通常需要更多token。

Conclusion: 这种内容无关的内省机制与哲学和心理学的领先理论一致，揭示了AI模型内省的局限性及其与人类认知的潜在相似性。

Abstract: Introspection is a foundational cognitive ability, but its mechanism is not well understood. Recent work has shown that AI models can introspect. We study their mechanism of introspection, first extensively replicating Lindsey et al. (2025)'s thought injection detection paradigm in large open-source models. We show that these models detect injected representations via two separable mechanisms: (i) probability-matching (inferring from perceived anomaly of the prompt) and (ii) direct access to internal states. The direct access mechanism is content-agnostic: models detect that an anomaly occurred but cannot reliably identify its semantic content. The two model classes we study confabulate injected concepts that are high-frequency and concrete (e.g., "apple'"); for them correct concept guesses typically require significantly more tokens. This content-agnostic introspective mechanism is consistent with leading theories in philosophy and psychology.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 实验结果表明，DPIP数据对现代LLM构成了挑战，它们在追踪任务进展和信念状态（belief state）方面表现不佳。

Conclusion: 当前LLM在处理涉及认知不对称的多模态协作任务时，难以有效推理命题内容和信念动态，而基于DEL的方法提供了另一种可行的建模路径。

Abstract: Establishing common ground, a shared set of beliefs and mutually recognized facts, is fundamental to collaboration, yet remains a challenge for current AI systems, especially in multimodal, multiparty settings, where the collaborators bring different information to the table. We introduce the Distributed Partial Information Puzzle (DPIP), a collaborative construction task that elicits rich multimodal communication under epistemic asymmetry. We present a multimodal dataset of these interactions, annotated and temporally aligned across speech, gesture, and action modalities to support reasoning over propositional content and belief dynamics. We then evaluate two paradigms for modeling common ground (CG): (1) state-of-the-art large language models (LLMs), prompted to infer shared beliefs from multimodal updates, and (2) an axiomatic pipeline grounded in Dynamic Epistemic Logic (DEL) that incrementally performs the same task. Results on the annotated DPIP data indicate that it poses a challenge to modern LLMs' abilities to track both task progression and belief state.

### [238] [Towards Provably Unbiased LLM Judges via Bias-Bounded Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05485)
*Benjamin Feuer,Lucas Rosenblatt,Oussama Elachqar*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出平均偏差有界性（A-BB）框架，确保LLM作为裁判时的偏差影响可控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着AI系统走向自主反馈循环，需要可验证的奖励机制；但在缺乏真值或存在未知/对抗性偏差时，现有LLM裁判系统无法提供强保证。

Method: 设计算法框架“平均偏差有界性”（A-BB），从理论上保证任何可测量的偏差都会导致危害/影响的减少，并验证其有效性。

Result: 在Arena-Hard-Auto数据集上测试四个LLM裁判，实现了(tau=0.5, delta=0.01)的偏差有界保证，同时在格式和结构偏差设置下保留了61-99%的原始排名相关性（多数组合超过80%）。

Conclusion: A-BB框架能够在不显著牺牲排名相关性的前提下，为LLM裁判系统提供严格的偏差控制保证，适用于高要求的自主AI场景。

Abstract: As AI models progress beyond simple chatbots into more complex workflows, we draw ever closer to the event horizon beyond which AI systems will be utilized in autonomous, self-maintaining feedback loops. Any autonomous AI system will depend on automated, verifiable rewards and feedback; in settings where ground truth is sparse or non-deterministic, one practical source of such rewards is an LLM-as-a-Judge. Although LLM judges continue to improve, the literature has yet to introduce systems capable of enforcing standards with strong guarantees, particularly when bias vectors are unknown or adversarially discovered. To remedy this issue, we propose average bias-boundedness (A-BB), an algorithmic framework which formally guarantees reductions of harm/impact as a result of any measurable bias in an LLM judge. Evaluating on Arena-Hard-Auto with four LLM judges, we achieve (tau=0.5, delta=0.01) bias-bounded guarantees while retaining 61-99% correlation with original rankings across formatting and schematic bias settings, with most judge-bias combinations exceeding 80%. The code to reproduce our findings is available at https://github.com/penfever/bias-bounded-evaluation.

</details>


### [239] [The Spike, the Sparse and the Sink: Anatomy of Massive Activations and Attention Sinks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05498)
*Shangwen Sun,Alfredo Canziani,Yann LeCun,Jiachen Zhu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了Transformer模型中“大规模激活”与“注意力汇”两个现象的共现主要是架构设计的人为产物，并阐明了二者各自独立的功能角色：前者作为全局隐式参数维持隐藏表示，后者作为局部机制调节注意力输出。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管先前的工作观察到大规模激活（massive activations）和注意力汇（attention sinks）经常同时出现且涉及相同的token，但它们在功能上的具体作用以及两者之间的因果关系尚不清楚。

Method: 通过系统的实验分析，研究人员对比了不同架构配置下的模型行为，特别是针对预归一化（pre-norm）配置的消融实验，以验证这两个现象是否由特定的架构选择导致其共现。

Result: 研究发现这两个现象的共现主要源于现代Transformer设计的架构伪影。大规模激活具有全局性，能诱导跨层持久的近乎恒定的隐藏表示，充当模型的隐式参数；而注意力汇具有局部性，调节各头的注意力输出并偏向短程依赖。当移除关键的预归一化配置时，这两个现象会发生解耦。

Conclusion: 大规模激活和注意力汇虽然常共同出现，但它们服务于相关但截然不同的功能，其共现并非必然，而是由预归一化这一关键架构选择所驱动。

Abstract: We study two recurring phenomena in Transformer language models: massive activations, in which a small number of tokens exhibit extreme outliers in a few channels, and attention sinks, in which certain tokens attract disproportionate attention mass regardless of semantic relevance. Prior work observes that these phenomena frequently co-occur and often involve the same tokens, but their functional roles and causal relationship remain unclear. Through systematic experiments, we show that the co-occurrence is largely an architectural artifact of modern Transformer design, and that the two phenomena serve related but distinct functions. Massive activations operate globally: they induce near-constant hidden representations that persist across layers, effectively functioning as implicit parameters of the model. Attention sinks operate locally: they modulate attention outputs across heads and bias individual heads toward short-range dependencies. We identify the pre-norm configuration as the key choice that enables the co-occurrence, and show that ablating it causes the two phenomena to decouple.

</details>

### [240] [HDLFORGE: A Two-Stage Multi-Agent Framework for Efficient Verilog Code Generation with Adaptive Model Escalation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04646)
*Armin Abdollahi,Saeid Shokoufa,Negin Ashrafi,Mehdi Kamal,Massoud Pedram*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: HDLFORGE 是一个两阶段多智能体框架，用于自动化生成 Verilog 代码，通过动态升级模型规模来优化生成速度与准确率的平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的单一阶段系统难以同时兼顾代码生成的速度和准确率，需要在两者之间做出妥协，且缺乏高效的错误检测与修复机制。

Method: 采用“紧凑编码器（中等规模LLM）+ 强编码器（超大规模LLM）”的两阶段架构；利用编译、Lint和冒烟测试等低成本诊断进行校准评分以触发升级；引入反例引导的形式化智能体，将有限模型检查轨迹转化为可复用的微测试，加速错误发现与修复；配备便携式升级控制器以兼容现有流水线。

Result: 在VerilogEval Human、V2及RTLLM基准测试中表现优异：HDLFORGE-Qwen在Human和V2数据集上Pass@1分别达到91.2%和91.8%，中位延迟降低约50%；在RTLLM上Pass@5达到97.2%，显著优于其他中等规模模型。

Conclusion: HDLFORGE 成功实现了准确性与延迟的更优权衡，证明了基于诊断评分的动态模型升级和形式化验证辅助修复策略在硬件描述语言生成任务中的有效性。

Abstract: We present HDLFORGE, a two-stage multi-agent framework for automated Verilog generation that optimizes the trade-off between generation speed and accuracy. The system uses a compact coder with a medium-sized LLM by default (Stage A) and escalates to a stronger coder with an ultra-large LLM (Stage B) only when needed, guided by a calibrated score from inexpensive diagnostics including compilation, lint, and smoke tests. A key innovation is a counterexample-guided formal agent that converts bounded-model-checking traces into reusable micro-tests, significantly reducing bug detection time and repair iterations. The portable escalation controller can wrap existing Verilog LLM pipelines without modifying their internals. Evaluated on VerilogEval Human, VerilogEval V2, and RTLLM benchmarks, HDLFORGE demonstrates improved accuracy-latency trade-offs compared to single-stage systems through comprehensive analysis of wall-clock time distributions, escalation thresholds, and agent ablations. On VerilogEval Human and VerilogEval V2, HDLFORGE-Qwen achieves 91.2% and 91.8% Pass@1 with roughly 50% lower median latency, dramatically improving accuracy over other medium-sized models, and 97.2% Pass@5 on RTLLM.

</details>


### [241] [Hardware-Software Co-design for 3D-DRAM-based LLM Serving Accelerator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04797)
*Cong Li,Yihan Yin,Chenhao Xue,Zhao Wang,Fujun Bai,Yixin Guo,Xiping Jiang,Qiang Wu,Yuan Xie,Guangyu Sun*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: Helios 是一种基于混合绑定的 LLM 服务加速器，旨在解决现有近存处理（NMP）设计在处理动态 LLM 负载时 KV 缓存管理粗糙和注意力执行流程僵化的问题。它通过设计片内执行流、片间通信原语及空间感知的 KV 缓存分配机制，实现了高效的分布式分块注意力执行，显著提升了速度和能效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 NMP 设计采用粗粒度的 KV 缓存管理和不灵活的注意力执行流程，无法有效应对 LLM 服务中高度动态的负载特性（如波动的请求到达率和可变的请求长度），限制了其加速能力。因此，需要一种能够弥合 LLM 服务中 KV 缓存动态性与 NMP 引擎间非均匀内存抽象之间差距的新架构。

Method: 提出 Helios 加速器，包含三个核心创新：1) 设计片内（intra-PE）执行流；2) 设计用于分布式分块注意力执行的片间（inter-PE）通信原语；3) 提出“空间感知”（spatially-aware）的 KV 缓存分配机制，以平衡注意力工作负载分布并最小化片间数据传输开销。

Result: 与现有的 GPU/NMP 设计相比，Helios 实现了 3.25 倍（几何平均）的速度提升和 3.36 倍（几何平均）的能效提升，同时将 P50/P99 令牌间时间延迟降低了 72%/76%。

Conclusion: Helios 通过创新的混合绑定架构和空间感知的资源管理机制，成功解决了 NMP 在动态 LLM 服务场景下的性能瓶颈，为高效、低延迟的生成式服务提供了新的硬件加速方案。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have been widely deployed for online generative services, where numerous LLM instances jointly handle workloads with fluctuating request arrival rates and variable request lengths. To efficiently execute coexisting compute-intensive and memory-intensive operators, near-memory processing (NMP) based computing paradigm has been extensively proposed. However, existing NMP designs adopt coarse-grained KV cache management and inflexible attention execution flow. Such limitations hinder these proposals from efficiently handling \textit{highly dynamic} LLM serving workloads, limiting their ability to accelerate LLM serving.
  To tackle these problems, we propose Helios, a Hybrid-bonding-based \uline{L}LM \uline{S}erving accelerator. Helios aims to bridge the fundamental gap between the dynamic nature of KV cache management in LLM serving and the distributed, non-uniform memory abstraction among NMP processing engines (PEs). To this end, we design both the intra-PE execution flow and the inter-PE communication primitives for distributed tiled attention execution. We further propose \textit{spatially-aware} KV cache allocation mechanism to balance the attention workload distribution while minimizing the inter-PE data transfer overhead. Compared with existing GPU/NMP designs, Helios achieves 3.25 times (geomean) speedup and 3.36 times (geomean) better energy efficiency, along with up to 72%/76% P50/P99 time-between-tokens degradation.

</details>


### [242] [VMXDOTP: A RISC-V Vector ISA Extension for Efficient Microscaling (MX) Format Acceleration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04979)
*Max Wipfli,Gamze İslamoğlu,Navaneeth Kunhi Purayil,Angelo Garofalo,Luca Benini*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 提出VMXDOTP，一种RISC-V向量ISA扩展，用于高效执行微缩放（MX）数据格式的点积运算，解决MX语义与向量执行不匹配的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代基于解码器的Transformer模型需要灵活加速器，而现有的微缩放（MX）数据格式虽然能减少数据量，但其块浮点表示和多步混合精度操作破坏了向量流水线的规则性，导致计算资源利用率低和性能下降。

Method: 设计并实现了一种名为VMXDOTP的RISC-V向量指令集架构（ISA）扩展，支持MXFP8和MXFP4输入、FP32和BF16累加以及软件定义的块大小，并将其集成到可扩展的共享L1内存向量处理单元（VPE）集群中。

Result: 在12nm FinFET工艺下，VMXDOTP增强的VPE集群实现了高达97%的MX-MatMul利用率；达到125 MXFP8-GFLOPS和250 MXFP4-GFLOPS的性能；能效分别达到843/1632 MXFP8/MXFP4-GFLOPS/W（1GHz, 0.8V）；面积开销仅为7.2%。相比软件模拟的MXFP8-MatMul，速度提升最高达7.0倍，能效提升4.9倍；相比现有MX引擎，面积效率提升1.4倍，能效提升2.1倍。

Conclusion: VMXDOTP通过硬件原语有效解决了微缩放格式在向量处理器上的执行效率问题，为现代Transformer模型的加速提供了高能效、高利用率的解决方案，显著优于软件模拟和现有专用引擎。

Abstract: Compared to the first generation of deep neural networks, dominated by regular, compute-intensive kernels such as matrix multiplications (MatMuls) and convolutions, modern decoder-based transformers interleave attention, normalization, and data-dependent control flow. This demands flexible accelerators, a requirement met by scalable, highly energy-efficient shared-L1-memory vector processing element (VPE) clusters. Meanwhile, the ever-growing size and bandwidth needs of state-of-the-art models make reduced-precision formats increasingly attractive. Microscaling (MX) data formats, based on block floating-point (BFP) representations, have emerged as a promising solution to reduce data volumes while preserving accuracy. However, MX semantics are poorly aligned with vector execution: block scaling and multi-step mixed-precision operations break the regularity of vector pipelines, leading to underutilized compute resources and performance degradation. To address these challenges, we propose VMXDOTP, a RISC-V Vector (RVV) 1.0 instruction set architecture (ISA) extension for efficient MX dot product execution, supporting MXFP8 and MXFP4 inputs, FP32 and BF16 accumulation, and software-defined block sizes. A VMXDOTP-enhanced VPE cluster achieves up to 97 % utilization on MX-MatMul. Implemented in 12 nm FinFET, it achieves up to 125 MXFP8-GFLOPS and 250 MXFP4-GFLOPS, with 843/1632 MXFP8/MXFP4-GFLOPS/W at 1 GHz, 0.8 V, and only 7.2 % area overhead. Our design yields up to 7.0x speedup and 4.9x energy efficiency with respect to software-emulated MXFP8-MatMul. Compared with prior MX engines, VMXDOTP supports variable block sizes, is up to 1.4x more area-efficient, and delivers up to 2.1x higher energy efficiency.

</details>


### [243] [Network Design for Wafer-Scale Systems with Wafer-on-Wafer Hybrid Bonding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05266)
*Patrick Iff,Tommaso Bonato,Maciej Besta,Luca Benini,Torsten Hoefler*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 本文研究了晶圆级集成中光刻掩膜版（reticle）的物理布局对网络拓扑和通信性能的影响，提出四种优化布局方案，显著提升了Transformer大模型的通信效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着芯片间通信带宽急剧下降，基于Transformer的大语言模型日益受到数据移动的限制。晶圆级集成通过混合键合技术提供超高速互连，但光刻掩膜版在晶圆上的物理位置直接影响网络拓扑结构和通信性能，需探索最优布局以缓解瓶颈。

Method: 从2D网格基线出发，提出四种光刻掩膜版布局策略：对齐（Aligned）、交错（Interleaved）、旋转（Rotated）和轮廓（Contoured），分析其对网络拓扑及通信性能的影响。

Result: 相较于基线，四种新布局将吞吐量最高提升250%，延迟降低36%，每字节传输能耗减少38%。

Conclusion: 合理设计光刻掩膜版在晶圆上的物理布局是优化晶圆级集成系统通信性能的关键，提出的四种布局方案为高性能AI硬件设计提供了有效途径。

Abstract: Transformer-based large language models are increasingly constrained by data movement as communication bandwidth drops sharply beyond the chip boundary. Wafer-scale integration using wafer-on-wafer hybrid bonding alleviates this limitation by providing ultra-high bandwidth between reticles on bonded wafers. In this paper, we investigate how the physical placement of reticles on wafers influences the achievable network topology and the resulting communication performance. Starting from a 2D mesh-like baseline, we propose four reticle placements (Aligned, Interleaved, Rotated, and Contoured) that improve throughput by up to 250%, reduce latency by up to 36%, and decrease energy per transmitted byte by up to 38%.

</details>


### [244] [NL2GDS: LLM-aided interface for Open Source Chip Design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05489)
*Max Eland,Jeyan Thiyagalingam,Dinesh Pamunuwa,Roshan Weerasekera*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: NL2GDS是一个利用大语言模型将自然语言硬件描述直接转换为可综合RTL和完整GDSII布局的新框架，通过OpenLane ASIC流程实现自动化设计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决日益复杂的硬件设计与高层规范及寄存器传输级（RTL）实现之间日益扩大的差距，从而阻碍快速原型设计和系统开发的问题。

Method: 采用模块化流水线：捕捉非正式的设计意图，利用多个LLM引擎生成HDL代码并进行验证，最后编排自动化的综合与布局流程，基于开源的OpenLane ASIC流完成从自然语言到GDSII的转换。

Result: 在ISCAS'85和ISCAS'89基准测试设计中，相比基线设计实现了高达36%的面积减少、35%的延迟降低以及70%的功耗节省。

Conclusion: 该框架展示了在民主化ASIC设计和加速硬件创新方面的巨大潜力。

Abstract: The growing complexity of hardware design and the widening gap between high-level specifications and register-transfer level (RTL) implementation hinder rapid prototyping and system design. We introduce NL2GDS (Natural Language to Layout), a novel framework that leverages large language models (LLMs) to translate natural language hardware descriptions into synthesizable RTL and complete GDSII layouts via the open-source OpenLane ASIC flow. NL2GDS employs a modular pipeline that captures informal design intent, generates HDL using multiple LLM engines and verifies them, and orchestrates automated synthesis and layout. Evaluations on ISCAS'85 and ISCAS'89 benchmark designs demonstrate up to 36% area reduction, 35% delay reduction, and 70% power savings compared to baseline designs, highlighting its potential to democratize ASIC design and accelerate hardware innovation.

### [245] [When Scaling Fails: Network and Fabric Effects on Distributed GPU Training Performance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04424)
*Dinesh Gopalan,Ratul Ali*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文通过实证研究揭示，分布式GPU训练在大规模扩展时性能收益递减，主要归因于常被忽略的网络拓扑、拥塞动态、集体同步行为和GPU局部性等因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决大型部署中普遍存在的性能收益递减和运行不稳定问题，探究导致扩展失败的根本原因，特别是高层训练框架常忽视的网络和硬件层效应。

Method: 对多个生产级集群上的分布式GPU训练性能进行广泛的实证研究，分析不同网络拓扑、运行时通信模式及硬件配置下的扩展特性。

Result: 发现网络拓扑、拥塞动态、集体同步行为及GPU局部性主导了多节点后的端到端训练性能；相同的模型和软件栈在不同硬件架构下表现出截然不同的扩展特征；识别出同步放大、拓扑诱导竞争和局部性驱动的性能差异等常见故障模式，且这些现象难以被标准分析工具捕获。

Conclusion: 提出了实用的诊断原则，帮助系统构建者理解扩展瓶颈、提高性能可预测性并降低大规模分布式训练的代价。

Abstract: Scaling distributed GPU training is commonly assumed to yield predictable performance gains as additional nodes are added. In practice, many large-scale deployments encounter diminishing returns and unstable behavior well before theoretical limits are reached. This paper examines why scaling fails in real systems, with a focus on the role of network and fabric effects that are often overlooked by higher-level training frameworks. We present an empirical study of distributed GPU training performance across multiple production-scale clusters. Our results show that network topology, congestion dynamics, collective synchronization behavior, and GPU locality frequently dominate end-to-end training performance once workloads move beyond a small number of nodes. Identical models and software stacks can exhibit sharply different scaling characteristics depending on fabric design and runtime communication patterns. We identify recurring failure modes that emerge as training transitions from single-node to multi-node execution, including synchronization amplification, topology-induced contention, and locality-driven performance variance. These effects are often invisible to standard profiling tools and are therefore misdiagnosed as framework or model-level inefficiencies. Based on these findings, we outline practical diagnostic principles that system builders can apply to understand scaling limits, improve predictability, and reduce the cost of large-scale distributed training.

### [246] [Auction-Based RIS Allocation With DRL: Controlling the Cost-Performance Trade-Off](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04433)
*Martin Mark Zan,Stefan Schwarz*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在下一代无线网络中，独立运营商部署的RIS资源稀缺且由多个基站竞争，需要一种可扩展、低开销且能公平高效分配这些资源的动态租赁机制。

Method: 采用同时递增拍卖格式让基站竞价获取边缘RIS；利用宏观信道参数估算效用以降低开销；引入深度强化学习（DRL）智能体优化竞价策略，并在预算约束下最大化性能；提出可调节参数以控制智能体的竞价激进程度。

Result: 仿真表明，基于RL的竞价策略显著优于启发式策略，实现了成本与频谱效率的最佳权衡；通过可调参数可灵活调控网络性能与支出之间的平衡。

Conclusion: 将拍卖分配机制与自适应强化学习相结合，是实现下一代无线网络中RIS高效、公平利用的有效途径。

Abstract: We study the allocation of reconfigurable intelligent surfaces (RISs) in a multi-cell wireless network, where base stations compete for control of shared RIS units deployed at the cell edges. These RISs, provided by an independent operator, are dynamically leased to the highest bidder using a simultaneously ascending auction format. Each base station estimates the utility of acquiring additional RISs based on macroscopic channel parameters, enabling a scalable and low-overhead allocation mechanism. To optimize the bidding behavior, we integrate deep reinforcement learning (DRL) agents that learn to maximize performance while adhering to budget constraints. Through simulations in clustered cell-edge environments, we demonstrate that reinforcement learning (RL)-based bidding significantly outperforms heuristic strategies, achieving optimal trade-offs between cost and spectral efficiency. Furthermore, we introduce a tunable parameter that governs the bidding aggressiveness of RL agents, enabling a flexible control of the trade-off between network performance and expenditure. Our results highlight the potential of combining auction-based allocation with adaptive RL mechanisms for efficient and fair utilization of RISs in next-generation wireless networks.

</details>

Result: 发现主要城市中心长期保留着遗留的2G/3G基础设施；存在大量未充分利用的塔站，具备成本节约潜力；识别出特定的“非4G需求区”，即活跃用户群仍由过时技术服务的区域；成功利用信号密度指标区分了绝对过载与局部拥塞。

By introducing a signal-density metric, we distinguish between absolute over-utilization and localized congestion. The results provide actionable intelligence for Mobile Network Operators (MNOs) to guide strategic LTE upgrades, optimize resource allocation, and bridge the digital divide in underserved regions.

### [248] [Arterial Network Traffic State Prediction with Connected Vehicle Data: An Abnormality-Aware Spatiotemporal Network](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04432)
*Lei Han,Mohamed Abdel-Aty,Yang-Jun Joo*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 提出基于网联车（CV）数据的城市干线交通预测框架，包含两阶段状态提取方法和异常感知时空图卷积网络（AASTGCN），在1050条路段的大规模真实网络中验证了有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于CV的干线交通预测研究多局限于仿真高渗透率场景或小规模网络，难以直接应用于现实世界的大规模城市干线网络。

Method: 1. 两阶段交通状态提取：从CV轨迹估算车辆级指标并聚合为网络级状态；2. AASTGCN模型：采用双专家架构分别建模正常与异常交通，结合时空GCN捕捉短时动态与长时周期性，并通过门控融合机制自适应平衡实时与历史信息。

Result: 在大规模真实路网中，该方法能有效提供实时链路级平均行程延误和排队长度等指标；AASTGCN在正常和异常交通条件下均优于现有模型；门控机制能根据交通状态自动调整历史周期信息与实时动态的权重。

Conclusion: 所提框架有效解决了CV数据在城市尺度干线网络中的应用难题，特别是通过分离建模异常交通显著提升了预测精度，为城市交通运行评估提供了可靠工具。

Abstract: Emerging connected-vehicle (CV) data shows great potential in urban traffic monitoring and forecasting. However, prior CV-based studies on arterial traffic measures prediction are limited to simulated high-penetration scenarios or small networks, which are challenging to apply in real-world city-scale arterial networks. To address such gaps, we develop a CV data-based arterial traffic prediction framework with two components: (1) a two-stage traffic state extraction method that estimates vehicle-level traffic measures from CV trajectories and then aggregates them into network-level traffic state measures; (2) an Abnormality-aware spatiotemporal graph convolution network (AASTGCN) that adopts a dual-expert architecture to separately model normal and abnormal traffic, and jointly captures short-term traffic dynamics and long-term periodicity via spatiotemporal GCN with a gated-fusion mechanism. Real-world CV data are used to test our method in a large arterial network with 1,050 links. Experimental results show that: 1) The proposed traffic estimation method is effective for large arterial networks to provide real-time traffic measures (e.g., link-level average travel delay and queue length), which are critical for urban traffic operation and evaluation. 2) Abnormal traffic prediction is typically challenging for existing methods. By modeling abnormal cases separately from normal traffic in two dedicated experts, AASTGCN outperforms existing models for both normal and abnormal traffic conditions. 3) The gate-fusion mechanism adaptively balances real-time and historical information: it leverages more historical-periodic information in normal traffic and shifts a higher weight to real-time traffic dynamics for abnormal traffic deviating abruptly from historical patterns.

</details>


### [249] [Periodic Scheduling of Grouped Time-Triggered Signals on a Single Resource](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04434)
*Josef Grus,Zdeněk Hanzálek,Claire Hanen*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文研究如何将时间触发信号分组为消息，并在单一资源上进行周期性调度，以平衡带宽利用率和调度灵活性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在汽车和航空等领域，短信号若单独发送会导致元数据（如消息ID）占用大量带宽，造成资源浪费；将多个信号组合成单条消息可提高链路利用率，但面临消息长度受限和调度灵活性下降的挑战。

Method: 提出一种针对时间触发信号分组与消息周期性调度的基础问题建模方法，探索在有限消息大小约束下实现高效资源利用的优化策略。

Result: 建立了信号分组与消息调度的联合优化模型，分析了消息长度对成功传输概率及调度灵活性的影响，并提出了相应的解决方案框架。

Conclusion: 合理的信号分组策略能显著提升通信资源利用率，但需在消息长度、传输可靠性和调度灵活性之间取得平衡，本文为该问题提供了理论基础和优化方向。

Abstract: Time-triggered messages are of crucial importance in modern communication networks. Offline-generated schedules, which specify start times for periodic messages, enable us to achieve deterministic behavior in critical applications. In automotive and avionics domains, so-called signals (measurements and commands) are periodically generated and communicated (via messages) among sensors, controllers, and actuators. However, the message contains not only the useful signal data, but also necessary metadata, e.g., message ID. Metadata is stored as a header or tail and extends the message size; when the signal is very short (as it often is in applications), sending each in a separate message is inefficient. Thus, several signals are grouped into a single message, depending on their periodicity and length, and sent with just one header. Such an approach increases the utilization of the communication resource (link or bus), since less bandwidth is wasted on headers (Kuaban et al. 2021). However, grouping the signals into messages is complicated. The maximum size of the message (including the metadata) is finite, since longer messages have a lower probability of successful delivery. Also, longer messages are less flexible for scheduling in a periodic setting. This is similar to the work of Huan et al. (2019), where the compromise between energy efficiency and latency for IoT devices was investigated. In this paper, we study the fundamental problem of grouping time-triggered signals into messages and periodic scheduling of messages on a single resource.

</details>

In this white paper, we present a detailed energy-efficiency characterization and modeling of a commercial O-RAN system based on comprehensive power and performance measurements, using a network deployment that faithfully replicates a production O-RAN network deployed by a wireless carrier. The results are drawn from an energy test campaign conducted through a joint collaboration between the Open RAN Center for Integration and Deployment (ORCID) Lab Testing and Evaluation (T&E) Project and the Open Networking Foundation / Rutgers WINLAB Energy Efficiency R&D project. The test environment includes an O-RAN system with an AWS-hosted O-CU, a dedicated-server O-DU, and six high-power, multi-band O-RUs. Our results identify the dominant factors influencing power consumption across the O-RAN stack and quantify energy usage variation under different operational and traffic scenarios. These measurements can be used by operators to parameterize power-consumption models, ultimately supporting data-driven energy optimization and more sustainable operation of commercial O-RAN networks.

### [251] [Towards Green Connectivity: An AI-Driven Mesh Architecture for Sustainable and Scalable Wireless Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04442)
*Muhammad Ahmed Mohsin,Muhammad Jazib,Muhammad Saad,Ayesha Mohsin*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有宏/微蜂窝基础设施存在严重低效：RF功率浪费近95%，在高密度临时场景（如朝觐）中需部署数千座柴油基站，消耗大量燃料并排放巨量CO2，且峰值需求下故障率高达40%。

Method: 提出三种集成使能技术：(1) 用户250-300米内部署低功耗节点，获得38 dB链路预算增益；(2) 将小区划分为多个非干扰区域以实现空间频率复用；(3) 利用LSTM预测未来5秒流量以优化资源分配。

Result: 系统级评估显示：有用能量交付提升84倍，部署成本降低74%，拥堵减少60%，容量提升近20倍，实现太阳能供电并消除柴油依赖。

Abstract: Traditional macro-cell and micro-cell infrastructures suffer from severe inefficiencies, with current macro-cell networks operating at less than 5 percent energy efficiency, leading to nearly 95 percent of RF power wasted in covering vacant areas. The problem becomes particularly acute in high-density scenarios such as the Hajj, where approximately 7,000 temporary diesel-powered towers are deployed each year, consuming 56 million liters of fuel and emitting around 148,000 tons of CO2, yet still experiencing failure rates of nearly 40 percent at peak demand. To overcome these limitations, we propose an AI-driven mesh architecture based on three integrated enablers: (i) proximity-based deployment of low-power nodes within 250 to 300 meters of users, yielding a 38 dB link-budget gain and up to 6000 times efficiency improvement; (ii) spatial frequency reuse, which partitions cells into multiple non-interfering zones and achieves nearly 20 times capacity gain; and (iii) predictive network intelligence leveraging LSTMs to forecast traffic 5 seconds ahead, enabling smarter allocation and reducing congestion by about 60 percent. System-level evaluations combining propagation modeling and validated link-budget analysis demonstrate that this architecture delivers up to an 84 times improvement in useful energy delivery, reduces deployment costs by nearly 74 percent, and eliminates diesel dependence through solar-powered operations, thereby enabling sustainable, green connectivity for both rural and ultra-dense urban environments.

### [252] [vLLM Semantic Router: Signal Driven Decision Routing for Mixture-of-Modality Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04444)
*Xunzhuo Liu,Huamin Chen,Samzong Lu,Yossi Ovadia,Guohong Wen,Zhengda Tan,Jintao Zhang,Senan Zedan,Yehudit Kerido,Liav Weiss,Bishen Yu,Asaad Balum,Noa Limoy,Abdallah Samara,Brent Salisbury,Hao Wu,Ryan Cook,Zhijie Wang,Qiping Pan,Rehan Khan,Avishek Goswami,Houston H. Zhang,Shuyi Wang,Ziang Tang,Fang Han,Zohaib Hassan,Jianqiao Zheng,Avinash Changrani*

TL;DR: vLLM Semantic Router 是一个信号驱动的决策路由框架，专为多模态混合模型（MoM）部署设计。它通过组合异构信号（启发式特征和神经分类器）并应用可配置的布尔规则，实现针对不同场景（如成本优化、隐私合规）的灵活路由，支持多提供商后端且无需修改代码。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大型语言模型在模态、能力和成本结构上的多样化，推理时如何选择最合适的模型进行请求路由已成为关键的系统挑战。现有方案难以同时满足多样化的部署需求（如多云企业、隐私监管、成本敏感等）。

Method: 提出“可组合的信号编排”机制：从请求中提取多种异构信号（包括毫秒级启发式特征和神经分类器），并通过可配置的布尔决策规则将其组合成特定的路由策略。利用十几种选择算法分析请求特征以寻找最具成本效益的模型，并通过插件链强制执行隐私和安全约束（如越狱检测、PII过滤、HaluGate幻觉检测）。

Result: 该架构支持 OpenAI API 标准，具备状态化多轮对话能力，并能跨多个异构后端（vLLM, OpenAI, Anthropic, Azure, Bedrock, Gemini, Vertex AI）进行多端点、多提供商的路由。作为 Envoy 外部处理器在生产环境中部署，证明了单一框架可通过配置差异化的成本、隐私和安全策略来服务多样化的部署场景。

Conclusion: 可组合的信号编排使得 vLLM Semantic Router 能够在一个统一的架构下，无需代码变更即可适应不同部署场景的需求，实现了高效、安全且灵活的模型路由解决方案。

Abstract: As large language models (LLMs) diversify across modalities, capabilities, and cost profiles, the problem of intelligent request routing -- selecting the right model for each query at inference time -- has become a critical systems challenge. We present vLLM Semantic Router, a signal-driven decision routing framework for Mixture-of-Modality (MoM) model deployments.
  The central innovation is composable signal orchestration: the system extracts heterogeneous signal types from each request -- from sub-millisecond heuristic features (keyword patterns, language detection, context length, role-based authorization) to neural classifiers (domain, embedding similarity, factual grounding, modality) -- and composes them through configurable Boolean decision rules into deployment-specific routing policies. Different deployment scenarios -- multi-cloud enterprise, privacy-regulated, cost-optimized, latency-sensitive -- are expressed as different signal-decision configurations over the same architecture, without code changes.
  Matched decisions drive semantic model routing: over a dozen of selection algorithms analyze request characteristics to find the best model cost-effectively, while per-decision plugin chains enforce privacy and safety constraints (jailbreak detection, PII filtering, hallucination detection via the three-stage HaluGate pipeline).
  The system provides OpenAI API support for stateful multi-turn conversations, multi-endpoint and multi-provider routing across heterogeneous backends (vLLM, OpenAI, Anthropic, Azure, Bedrock, Gemini, Vertex AI), and a pluggable authorization factory supporting multiple auth providers. Deployed in production as an Envoy external processor, the architecture demonstrates that composable signal orchestration enables a single routing framework to serve diverse deployment scenarios with differentiated cost, privacy, and safety policies.

</details>


### [253] [Dynamic Model Routing and Cascading for Efficient LLM Inference: A Survey](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04445)
*Yasmin Moslem,John D. Kelleher*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型（LLM）能力、成本和领域差异巨大，静态部署无法根据查询复杂度和领域自适应选择模型，导致性能次优且成本高昂，亟需智能推理时模型选择机制。

Method: 对最先进的多LLM路由和级联方法进行系统性分析，涵盖查询难度、人类偏好、聚类、不确定性量化、强化学习、多模态及级联等多种范式；提出一个从决策时机、信息使用和计算方法三个维度刻画路由系统的概念框架。

Result: 有效的多LLM路由需在竞争目标间取得平衡，最佳策略取决于部署和计算约束；精心设计的路由系统能通过战略性地利用各模型的专业能力并最大化效率增益，其表现甚至优于单一最强模型。

Conclusion: 尽管动态路由系统显著提升了效率和性能，但在开发能够跨越不同架构、模态和应用场景的通用路由机制方面仍面临开放挑战。

Abstract: The rapid growth of large language models (LLMs) with diverse capabilities, costs, and domains has created a critical need for intelligent model selection at inference time. While smaller models suffice for routine queries, complex tasks demand more capable models. However, static model deployment does not account for the complexity and domain of incoming queries, leading to suboptimal performance and increased costs. Dynamic routing systems that adaptively select models based on query characteristics have emerged as a solution to this challenge.
  We provide a systematic analysis of state-of-the-art multi-LLM routing and cascading approaches. In contrast to mixture-of-experts architectures, which route within a single model, we study routing across multiple independently trained LLMs. We cover diverse routing paradigms, including query difficulty, human preferences, clustering, uncertainty quantification, reinforcement learning, multimodality, and cascading. For each paradigm, we analyze representative methods and examine key trade-offs. Beyond taxonomy, we introduce a conceptual framework that characterizes routing systems along three dimensions: when decisions are made, what information is used, and how they are computed. This perspective highlights that practical systems are often compositional, integrating multiple paradigms under operational constraints.
  Our analysis demonstrates that effective multi-LLM routing requires balancing competing objectives. Choosing the optimal routing strategy depends on deployment and computational constraints. Well-designed routing systems can outperform even the most powerful individual models by strategically leveraging specialized capabilities across models while maximizing efficiency gains. Meanwhile, open challenges remain in developing routing mechanisms that generalize across diverse architectures, modalities, and applications.

### [254] [Threadle: A Memory-Efficient Network Storage and Query Engine for Large, Multilayer, and Mixed-mode Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04446)
*Carl Nordlund,Yukun Jiao*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: Threadle是一个开源的高性能、内存高效的网络存储和查询引擎，专为处理行政登记数据生成的超大规模多模态网络而设计。其核心创新在于伪投影技术，允许在不实际构建内存占用巨大的单模态投影的情况下查询双模态（二分）数据层。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有网络库无法高效处理大规模的双模态（二分）数据。由行政登记数据生成的全人口网络通常包含数百万个节点和数十亿条边，属于超大规模、多层、混合模式网络，传统方法在内存和处理效率上存在根本性局限。

Method: 采用伪投影（pseudo-projection）方法，将双模态层作为单模态形式进行查询，但从不实际生成内存不可接受的投影结果。该系统基于C#编写，提供原生支持多层混合模式网络的功能，集成节点属性管理器，并配备包含50多个命令的CLI前端用于网络构建、处理和管理。此外，还配套了threadleR R语言前端以支持高级采样和遍历分析。

Result: 实验证明，Threadle能够以约20GB的RAM存储包含2000万个节点的网络，该网络等效于8万亿条投影边，压缩比超过2000:1，远超实体化投影的存储需求。系统成功实现了对极大规模异构网络的存储与高效查询。

Conclusion: Threadle通过伪投影技术有效解决了超大规模双模态网络的处理瓶颈，提供了内存效率和查询性能的显著突破，为全人口网络分析提供了强大的工具支持。

Abstract: We present Threadle, an open-source, high-performance, and memory-efficient network storage and query engine written in C#. Designed for working with full-population networks derived from administrative register data, which represent very large, multilayer, mixed-mode networks with millions of nodes and billions of edges, Threadle addresses a fundamental limitation of existing network libraries: the inability to efficiently handle two-mode (bipartite) data at scale. Threadle's core innovation is a pseudo-projection approach that allows two-mode layers to be queried as if they were projected into one-mode form, without ever materializing the memory-prohibitive projection. We demonstrate that a network with 20 million nodes containing layers equivalent to 8 trillion projected edges can be stored in approximately 20 GB of RAM -- a compression ratio exceeding 2000:1 compared to materialized projection. Additionally, Threadle provides native support for multilayer mixed-mode networks, an integrated node attribute manager, and a CLI frontend with 50+ commands for the construction, processing, file handling, and management of very large heterogeneous networks. Threadle is freely available at https://www.threadle.dev and can either be obtained as precompiled binaries for Win, macOS and Linux, or compiled directly from source. Supplementing Threadle is threadleR, an R frontend that enables advanced sampling- and traversal-based analyses on very large, heterogeneous, multilayer, mixed-mode population-scale networks.

Abstract: This paper investigates the integration of large language models (LLMs) as reasoning agents in repeated spectrum auctions within heterogeneous networks (HetNets). While auction-based mechanisms have been widely employed for efficient resource allocation, most prior works assume one-shot auctions, static bidder behavior, and idealized conditions. In contrast to traditional formulations where base station (BS) association and power allocation are centrally optimized, we propose a distributed auction-based framework in which each BS independently conducts its own multi-channel auction, and user equipments (UEs) strategically decide both their association and bid values. Within this setting, UEs operate under budget constraints and repeated interactions, transforming resource allocation into a long-term economic decision rather than a one-shot optimization problem. The proposed framework enables the evaluation of diverse bidding behaviors -from classical myopic and greedy policies to LLM-based agents capable of reasoning over historical outcomes, anticipating competition, and adapting their bidding strategy across episodes. Simulation results reveal that the LLM-empowered UE consistently achieves higher channel access frequency and improved budget efficiency compared to benchmarks. These findings highlight the potential of reasoning-enabled agents in future decentralized wireless networks markets and pave the way for lightweight, edge-deployable LLMs to support intelligent resource allocation in next-generation HetNets.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 边缘设备AI应用激增需要高效的传输协议；现有Multipath TCP的内核拥塞控制缺乏灵活性和可编程性；网络状态测量噪声导致部分可观测，挑战数据驱动方法（如DRL）。

Method: 提出基于Transformer的拥塞控制优化(TCCO)框架：采用解耦架构，通过轻量级内核客户端和用户空间代理将控制决策卸载到外部决策引擎；使用基于Transformer的DRL智能体，利用自注意力机制捕捉时间依赖、过滤噪声并协调子流。

Result: 在模拟环境和真实双频Wi-Fi测试床上的广泛评估表明，TCCO相比最先进基线具有更优越的适应性和性能。

Abstract: The proliferation of artificial intelligence applications on edge devices necessitates efficient transport protocols that leverage multi-homed connectivity across heterogeneous networks. While Multipath TCP enables bandwidth aggregation, its in-kernel congestion control mechanisms lack the programmability and flexibility needed for achieving efficient transmission. Additionally, inherent measurement noise renders network state partially observable, challenging data-driven approaches like deep reinforcement learning (DRL). To address these challenges, we propose a Transformer-based Congestion Control Optimization (TCCO) framework for multipath transport. TCCO employs a decoupled architecture that offloads control decisions to an external decision engine via a lightweight in-kernel client and user-space proxy, enabling edge devices to leverage external computational resources while maintaining TCP/IP compatibility. The Transformer-based DRL agent in the external decision engine uses self-attention to capture temporal dependencies, filter noise, and coordinate control across subflows through a unified policy. Extensive evaluation on both simulated and real dual-band Wi-Fi testbeds demonstrates that TCCO achieves superior adaptability and performance than state-of-the-art baselines, validating the feasibility and effectiveness of TCCO for wireless networks.

This demonstration introduces two key technologies: Meander NFC and picoRing NFC. First, Meander NFC expands a clothing-based NFC networking area up to body scale while enabling a stable readout of small NFC tags occupying 1% of the coverage area. Meander NFC uses a meander coil which creates a spatially confined inductive field along the textile surface, ensuring robust coupling with small tags while preventing undesired electromagnetic body coupling. Second, picoRing NFC solves the weak inductive coupling caused by distance and size mismatches. By leveraging middle-range NFC and coil optimization, picoRing NFC extends the communication range to connect these disparate nodes between the ring and wristband.

### [259] [Adaptive Personalized Federated Reinforcement Learning for RIS-Assisted Aerial Relays in SAGINs with Fluid Antennas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04788)
*Yuxuan Yang,Bin Lyu,Abbas Jamalipour*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文针对天地空一体化网络（SAGIN）中因跨层设施与增强技术紧密集成导致的动态性和异构性挑战，提出了一种结合RIS辅助无人机中继和低轨卫星星座的架构。该架构同时服务具备流体天线系统（FAS）和传统天线的用户。通过建立包含卫星移动、无人机轨迹、RIS相位控制及用户异构接收能力的系统模型，将多热点下行速率最大化问题建模为分层Stackelberg博弈，并提出自适应个性化联邦强化学习（FRL）算法，以联合优化无人机轨迹和RIS相位控制。仿真结果表明，该方法在动态异构环境中具有优越性能，验证了个性化策略的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着低轨卫星、无人机（UAV）和地面设备的深度集成，以及可重构智能表面（RIS）和流体天线系统（FAS）等增强技术的应用，天地空一体化网络（SAGIN）面临显著的环境动态性和异构性挑战。这些特性使得传统的大规模SAGIN系统建模与优化方法难以奏效，亟需新的机制来应对复杂的跨层交互和实时变化的信道环境。

Method: 1. 构建系统模型：显式刻画低轨卫星（LEO）星座的移动性、无人机轨迹、RIS相位控制以及FAS与传统用户的异构接收能力。
2. 问题建模：将多热点下行速率最大化问题转化为分层Stackelberg博弈问题，分析其可解性。
3. 算法设计：提出一种自适应个性化联邦强化学习（FRL）算法，用于在异质且时变的多热点环境中自适应地优化无人机轨迹和RIS相位控制。

Result: 仿真结果显示，所提出的自适应个性化联邦强化学习算法在多热点下行速率方面表现优异。该算法能够有效适应动态变化的异构环境，且“个性化”策略在不同热点场景下显著提升了系统性能，验证了该方法在处理复杂SAGIN场景中的有效性。

Conclusion: 通过将RIS和FAS技术融入SAGIN架构，并结合分层博弈理论与个性化联邦强化学习，可以有效解决大规模网络中的动态性与异构性难题。研究证明了自适应个性化策略在优化无人机路径规划和RIS波束成形方面的关键作用，为未来灵活通用的天地空一体化网络提供了可行的解决方案。

Abstract: Space-air-ground integrated networks (SAGINs) interconnect satellites, uncrewed aerial vehicles (UAVs), and ground devices to enable flexible and ubiquitous wireless services. The integration of reconfigurable intelligent surfaces (RISs) and fluid antenna systems (FASs) further enhances radio environment controllability. However, the tight integration of cross-layer facilities and radio enhancement technologies leads to pronounced environmental dynamics and heterogeneity, posing fundamental challenges for system modeling and optimization in large-scale SAGINs. This paper investigates a SAGIN in which low Earth orbit (LEO) satellite constellations communicate with multiple ground hotspots via RIS-assisted UAV relays, serving both FAS-equipped and conventional users. A system model is developed that explicitly captures satellite mobility, UAV trajectories, RIS phase control, and heterogeneous user reception capabilities. Accordingly, a multi-hotspot downlink rate maximization problem is studied, whose solvability is analyzed through a hierarchical Stackelberg game. To address heterogeneous and time-varying multi-hotspot environments, an adaptive personalized federated reinforcement learning (FRL) algorithm is proposed for adaptive optimization of UAV trajectories and RIS phase controls. Simulation results demonstrate superior performance and validate the effectiveness of personalization in dynamic heterogeneous SAGIN scenarios.

</details>


### [260] [Analysis of Proactive Uncoordinated Techniques to Mitigate Interference in FMCW Automotive Radars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04944)
*Alessandro Bazzi,Francesco Miccoli,Fabrizio Cuccoli,Luca Facheris,Vincent Martinez*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文研究了全频段FMCW雷达在密集交通场景下的互干扰问题，评估了三种无需车际协调的主动抗干扰方法（帧级跳频、啁啾级跳频、基于指南针的方向性方法）的有效性。结果显示，密集场景下故障风险高，其中“啁啾级频率跳频+大带宽”组合效果最佳，而指南针法性价比低。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着现代车辆广泛采用毫米波雷达作为ADAS核心传感器，同频段内雷达数量激增导致严重的互干扰问题，可能引发系统故障和安全隐患。现有研究缺乏对全车配备FMCW雷达场景下，不同无协调抗干扰策略的系统性效能评估。

Method: 构建了一个新型仿真模型，模拟真实道路交通场景，能够捕捉相关干扰并考虑主要雷达设置参数。研究对比了三种抗干扰方案：(i) 帧级随机载波频率跳变；(ii) 啁啾级随机载波频率跳变；(iii) 基于指南针的方向性抗干扰法（可与前两者结合）。通过计算概率失效指标来量化各方法对直接信号和反射信号干扰的缓解能力。

Result: 1. 密集交通场景下雷达故障风险显著升高。2. 在所有测试方法中，“啁啾级频率跳频”配合足够大的工作带宽是缓解干扰最有效的手段。3. 基于指南针的方向性方法效果有限，其增加的复杂性与其带来的性能提升不成正比。4. 帧级跳频的效果次之，且不如啁啾级跳频稳健。

Conclusion: 为确保FMCW雷达系统在密集交通环境中的可靠性，应优先采用啁啾级频率跳变技术并扩展带宽。基于方向性的指南针辅助抗干扰策略由于增益不明显，不建议在资源受限或追求高性价比的系统部署中使用。未来设计需重点关注无需通信协作的抗干扰算法优化。

Abstract: Modern vehicles increasingly rely on advanced driver-assistance systems (ADAS), with radars playing a key role due to their cost-effectiveness and reliable performance. However, the growing number of radars operating in the same spectrum raises concerns about mutual interference, which could lead to system malfunctions and potential safety risks. This study focuses on a scenario in which all vehicles are equipped with frequency-modulated continuous-wave (FMCW) radars, and it assesses the impact of interference on radar functionality - expressed in terms of probability of failure - by considering both direct and reflected signals. The radars may employ one of the following proactive mitigation methods to reduce the impact of interference, all of which require no inter-vehicle coordination but differ in complexity: (i) random carrier-frequency hopping on a frame-by-frame basis, (ii) random carrier-frequency hopping on a chirp-by-chirp basis, and (iii) a directional, compass-based method specifically addressing interference from opposite directions, which can be combined with either of the two previous methods. In this work, we assume realistic simulated road traffic scenarios and develop a novel model that captures correlated interference and accounts for the main radar setting parameters. Results reveal that dense scenarios pose a high risk of radar malfunctions. Among the analyzed methods, chirp-by-chirp frequency hopping emerges as the most effective approach to mitigate interference and ensure system reliability, but only when combined with a sufficiently large bandwidth. The compass-based method, on the other hand, shows limited effectiveness and appears not worth the additional system complexity.

</details>


### [261] [V2N-Based Algorithm and Communication Protocol for Autonomous Non-Stop Intersections](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05165)
*Lorenzo Farina,Lorenzo Mario Amorosa,Marco Rapelli,Barbara Maví Masini,Claudio Casetti,Alessandro Bazzi*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: Moveover是一种新型自动驾驶交叉路口管理算法，通过V2N通信协议让车辆无需停车即可连续通过路口。该算法将轨迹和速度规划分配给单车进行优化，并由局部控制器负责冲突区预订以防止碰撞。在理想和非理想网络条件下（模拟4G/5G延迟）的仿真显示，Moveover在行程时间和污染物排放方面显著优于基线策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自动驾驶交叉路口管理方案存在两个主要问题：一是过度依赖计算密集型集中式控制器，二是忽视了现实世界通信网络的实际限制（如延迟）。这导致方案在实际部署中效率低下或不可行。

Method: 提出Moveover算法，包含以下核心机制：1) 基于车网(V2N)通信协议；2) 去中心化决策：每辆网联自动驾驶汽车(CAV)根据自身运动学特性独立优化轨迹和速度曲线；3) 局部冲突解决：由路口本地控制器执行确定性的冲突区域预订以预防碰撞。评估场景涵盖单车道、多车道及环岛布局，并测试了真实城市地图上的多个路口，同时模拟了4G和5G通信延迟。

Result: 在多种路口布局和不同网络条件（包括模拟4G/5G延迟）下的仿真结果表明，Moveover算法显著优于现有的基线策略。具体表现为大幅缩短车辆通行时间，并有效降低了污染物排放。

Conclusion: Moveover算法通过结合单车智能优化与局部集中式冲突协调，成功解决了现有方案对高算力集中控制的依赖及对网络现实的忽视问题。该算法证明了在无停车情况下实现高效、安全且环保的自动驾驶交叉路口通行是可行的，即使在非理想的通信网络环境下也能保持优越性能。

Abstract: Intersections are critical areas for road safety and traffic efficiency, accounting for a significant portion of vehicle crashes and fatalities. While connected and autonomous vehicle (CAV) technologies offer a promising solution for autonomous intersection management, many existing proposals either rely on computationally heavy centralized controllers or overlook the practical impairments of real-world communication networks. This paper introduces seamless mobility of vehicles over intersections (Moveover), a novel algorithm comprising a vehicle-to-network (V2N) communication protocol designed to let vehicles cross autonomous intersections without stopping. Moveover delegates trajectory and speed profile selection to individual vehicles, allowing each CAV to optimize them according to its unique kinematic characteristics. Simultaneously, a local intersection controller prevents collisions through deterministic conflict zone reservations. The algorithm is rigorously evaluated under both ideal and non-ideal networking conditions, specifically modeling 4G and 5G communication delays, across multiple layouts including single-lane, multi-lane, and roundabouts. Furthermore, we test Moveover on a real urban map with multiple intersections. Simulation results demonstrate that Moveover significantly outperforms baseline strategies, offering substantial improvements in travel times and reduced pollutant emissions.

</details>
